Built with Alectryon, running Coq+SerAPI v8.20.0+0.20.0. Bubbles () indicate interactive fragments: hover for details, tap to reveal contents. Use Ctrl+↑ Ctrl+↓ to navigate, Ctrl+🖱️ to focus. On Mac, use ⌘ instead of Ctrl.
(************************************************************************

 Grothendieck construction: fibrations to pseudofunctors

 The Grothendieck construction gives a biequivalence between the
 bicategory of fibrations over a fixed category `C` and the bicategory
 of indexed categories over `C`. To construct this biequivalence, we
 need to construct the following:
 1. A pseudofunctor from the bicategory of fibrations to the bicategory
    of pseudofunctors
 2. A pseudofunctor from the bicategory of pseudofunctors to the
    bicategory of fibrations
 3. The unit and a proof that it is a pointwise adjoint equivalence
 4. The counit and a proof that it is a pointwise adjoint equivalence

 In this file, we construct the first part of this biequivalence (a
 pseudofunctor from fibrations to pseudofunctors). This construction
 mainly recollects statements that are already present in UniMath.

 There are a couple of ideas behind this formalization. First of all,
 for the Grothendieck construction, we are only interested in a rather
 particular class of pseudofunctors, namely those pseudofunctors for
 which the domain is a discrete bicategory (i.e., a category). This
 allows us to simplify some of the coherences of pseudofunctors, which
 is done in the file `PseudoTransformationIntoCat.v`. Second of all, we
 explicitly use the notion of indexed categories (see the directory
 `IndexedCategories` in `CategoryTheory`) for this construction, because
 this allows us to formulate the fundamental constructions purely in the
 language of category theory and without mentioning bicategories.

 Contents
 1. Preservation of the identity
 2. Preservation of composition
 3. The data
 4. The laws
 5. Pseudofunctor from fibrations to pseudofunctors

 ************************************************************************)

     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) f

   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y) f
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y)))
  (transportb (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) (HD x y f xx))
     (id_left (id₁ y)) (id_disp (HD x y f xx)) ;; 
   HD x y f xx)%mor_disp =
transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
  (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) f
     (id_right (id₁ y)))
  (cartesian_factorisation (HD x y f xx) (id₁ y)
     (transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
        (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
        (HD x y f xx ;; id_disp xx)) ;; cartesian_factorisation
                                          (disp_functor_identity_is_cartesian_disp_functor
                                             D x y f
                                             xx
                                             (HD x y f
                                                xx)

                                                xx)

                                                xx))

   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y) f
     (! id_left (id₁ y)) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) f
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (! id_left (id₁ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y) f
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y)))
  (HD x y f xx)

  (cleaving_to_indexed_cat D HD) x
transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
  (maponpaths (compose (id₁ y))
     (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f) @
   assoc (id₁ y) (id₁ y) f @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) f
     (id_right (id₁ y)))
  (transportf (mor_disp (HD x y f xx) xx)
     (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
     (HD x y f xx ;; id_disp xx)%mor_disp) =

  (! id_left f @

     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) f
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (! id_left (id₁ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y) f
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y)))
  (HD x y f xx)

   (id_right f @ ! id_left f) @

     (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f) @

     (id_right (id₁ y))) (HD x y f xx) =

  (! id_left f @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y) f
     (! id_left (id₁ y)) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) f

C: category
D: disp_univalent_category C
HD: cleaving D
x, y: cat_to_bicat (C ^opp)
f: cat_to_bicat (C ^opp) ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: indexed_cat_to_psfunctor
  (cleaving_to_indexed_cat D HD) x
! id_right f @
(id_right f @ ! id_left f) @
maponpaths (compose (id₁ y))
  (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f) @
assoc (id₁ y) (id₁ y) f @
cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) f
  (id_right (id₁ y)) =
! id_left f @
cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y) f
  (! id_left (id₁ y)) @
cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
  (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) f
  (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y) (! id_left (id₁ y))) @
cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
  f
  (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y))

  apply homset_property.
Qed.

C: category
D₁, D₂, D₃: disp_univalent_category C
HD₁: cleaving D₁
HD₂: cleaving D₂
HD₃: cleaving D₃
F: cartesian_disp_functor (functor_identity C) D₁ D₂
G: cartesian_disp_functor (functor_identity C) D₂ D₃
x, y: cat_to_bicat (C ^opp)
f: cat_to_bicat (C ^opp) ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: indexed_cat_to_psfunctor
  (cleaving_to_indexed_cat D₁ HD₁) x
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx)))) (id_right (id₁ y))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
        (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx)))) (id_right (id₁ y))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
           (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx))))
        (id_right (id₁ y))
        (transportf
           (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
              (G y (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))))
           (id_right (id₁ y))
           (transportf
              (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
                 (G y (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))))
              (id_right (id₁ y))
              (id_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx))) ;; 
               cartesian_factorisation
                 (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian
                    G (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))) (id₁ y)
                 (transportf
                    (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
                     HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[
                     z] G x (F x xx))
                    (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
                       f) (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx))))) ;; 
            id_disp (G y (HD₂ x y f (F x xx)))) ;; 
         ♯ G
           (cartesian_factorisation
              (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian F
                 (HD₁ x y f xx)) (id₁ y)
              (transportf
                 (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
                  HD₂ x y f (F x xx) -->[ z] F x xx)
                 (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
                    f) (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))))) ;; 
      id_disp (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx)))) ;; id_disp
                                               (G y
                                                 (F y
                                                 (HD₁
                                                 x y f
                                                 xx))))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx)))) (id_right (id₁ y))
  (cartesian_factorisation (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
           (G x (F x xx))) (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) ;; id_disp
                                       (G x (F x xx)))) ;; 
   cartesian_factorisation
     (disp_functor_over_id_composite_is_cartesian
        (pr2 F) (pr2 G) x y f xx (HD₁ x y f xx)
        (HD₁ x y f xx) (HD₁ x y f xx)) (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
         HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[ z] G x (F x xx))
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))))%mor_disp

  
C: category
D₁, D₂, D₃: disp_univalent_category C
HD₁: cleaving D₁
HD₂: cleaving D₂
HD₃: cleaving D₃
F: cartesian_disp_functor (functor_identity C) D₁ D₂
G: cartesian_disp_functor (functor_identity C) D₂ D₃
x, y: cat_to_bicat (C ^opp)
f: cat_to_bicat (C ^opp) ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: indexed_cat_to_psfunctor
  (cleaving_to_indexed_cat D₁ HD₁) x
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx)))) (id_right (id₁ y))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
        (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx))))
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
           (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx))))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
              (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))))
        (transportf
           (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
              (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx))))
           (cancel_postcomposition
              (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
              (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
              (cancel_postcomposition
                 (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
                 (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
                 (cancel_postcomposition
                    (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id₁ y)
                    (id_right (id₁ y)))))
           (transportf
              (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
                 (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx))))
              (cancel_postcomposition
                 (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y
                  · id₁ y)
                 (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
                 (id₁ y)
                 (cancel_postcomposition
                    (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
                    (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
                    (cancel_postcomposition
                       (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
                       (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
                       (cancel_postcomposition
                          (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
                          (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))))))
              (id_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx))) ;; 
               cartesian_factorisation
                 (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian
                    G (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))) (id₁ y)
                 (transportf
                    (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
                     HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[
                     z] G x (F x xx))
                    (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
                       f) (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))) ;; 
               id_disp (G y (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))) ;; 
               ♯ G
                 (cartesian_factorisation
                    (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian
                       F (HD₁ x y f xx)) (id₁ y)
                    (transportf
                       (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
                        HD₂ x y f (F x xx) -->[
                        z] F x xx)
                       (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
                          f) (HD₂ x y f (F x xx)))) ;; 
               id_disp (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx))) ;; 
               id_disp (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx))))%mor_disp)))) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx)))) (id_right (id₁ y))
  (cartesian_factorisation (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
           (G x (F x xx))) (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) ;; id_disp
                                       (G x (F x xx)))) ;; 
   cartesian_factorisation
     (disp_functor_over_id_composite_is_cartesian
        (pr2 F) (pr2 G) x y f xx (HD₁ x y f xx)
        (HD₁ x y f xx) (HD₁ x y f xx)) (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
         HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[ z] G x (F x xx))
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))))%mor_disp

           (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
              (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)))) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y))
  (cartesian_factorisation
     (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian G
        (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))) (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
         HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[ z] G x (F x xx))
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))) ;; id_disp
                                         (G y
                                            (HD₂ x y f
                                               (F x xx))) ;;

     (cartesian_factorisation

                                       (G y
                                          (F y
                                             (HD₁ x y
                                                f xx))) ;; 
   id_disp (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx))))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx)))) (id_right (id₁ y))

        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) ;; id_disp
                                       (G x (F x xx)))) ;;

     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y)
              (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
              (! id_left (id₁ y))))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
              (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)))) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
        (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx))))
     (! id_right (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y))
     (cartesian_factorisation
        (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian G
           (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))) (id₁ y)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
            HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[
            z] G x (F x xx))
           (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
           (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))) ;; id_disp
                                            (G y
                                               (HD₂ x
                                                 y f
                                                 (F x
                                                 xx))) ;; 
      ♯ G
        (cartesian_factorisation
           (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian F
              (HD₁ x y f xx)) (id₁ y)
           (transportf
              (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
               HD₂ x y f (F x xx) -->[ z] F x xx)
              (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
              (HD₂ x y f (F x xx)))))%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (G y (F y (HD₁ x y f xx)))) (id_right (id₁ y))
  (cartesian_factorisation (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (id₁ y)

           (G x (F x xx))) (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) ;; id_disp
                                       (G x (F x xx)))) ;; 
   cartesian_factorisation
     (disp_functor_over_id_composite_is_cartesian
        (pr2 F) (pr2 G) x y f xx (HD₁ x y f xx)
        (HD₁ x y f xx) (HD₁ x y f xx)) (id₁ y)

        (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
         HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[ z] G x (F x xx))
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))))%mor_disp

        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) ;; id_disp
                                       (G x (F x xx)))) ;; 
   cartesian_factorisation
     (disp_functor_over_id_composite_is_cartesian
        (pr2 F) (pr2 G) x y f xx (HD₁ x y f xx)
        (HD₁ x y f xx) (HD₁ x y f xx)) (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
         HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[ z] G x (F x xx))
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))))%mor_disp

                 (! id_left (id₁ y))))) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition
              (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
              (id₁ y)
              (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
                 (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))))) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
              (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)))) @
      cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))) @
      cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y)))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
        (pr1 G x (pr1 F x xx)))
     (assoc (id₁ y) (id₁ y) f)
     (cartesian_factorisation
        (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian G
           (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))) (id₁ y)
        (transportf
           (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
            HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[
            z] G x (F x xx))
           (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
           (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))) ;; (♯ G
                                             (cartesian_factorisation
                                                (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian
                                                 F
                                                 (HD₁
                                                 x y f
                                                 xx))
                                                (id₁ y)
                                                (transportf
                                                 (λ 
                                                 z : 
                                                 C
                                                 ⟦ y,
                                                 x ⟧,
                                                 HD₂ x
                                                 y f
                                                 (F x
                                                 xx) -->[
                                                 z] 
                                                 F x
                                                 xx)
                                                 (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof
                                                 f)
                                                 (HD₂
                                                 x y f
                                                 (F x
                                                 xx)))) ;; 
                                           ♯ (pr1 G)
                                             (♯ (pr1 F)
                                                (HD₁ x
                                                 y f
                                                 xx))))%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (pr1 G x (pr1 F x xx)))
  (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) f
     (id_right (id₁ y)))
  (cartesian_factorisation (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
           (G x (F x xx))) (id_right f @ ! id_left f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) ;; id_disp
                                       (G x (F x xx)))) ;; 
   cartesian_factorisation
     (disp_functor_over_id_composite_is_cartesian
        (pr2 F) (pr2 G) x y f xx (HD₁ x y f xx)
        (HD₁ x y f xx) (HD₁ x y f xx)) (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
         HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[ z] G x (F x xx))

        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))) ;; ♯ (pr1 G)
                                         (♯ (pr1 F)
                                            (HD₁ x y f
                                               xx)))%mor_disp

        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition
              (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
              (id₁ y)
              (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
                 (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))))) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
              (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)))) @
      cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))) @
      cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y)))
  (cartesian_factorisation
     (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian G
        (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))) (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
         HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[ z] G x (F x xx))
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))) ;; transportf
                                         (mor_disp
                                            (G y
                                               (HD₂ x
                                                 y f

                                                 x xx)))

  (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (pr1 G x (pr1 F x xx)))
  (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) f
     (id_right (id₁ y)))

                                       (G x (F x xx)))) ;;

      cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y)))
  (cartesian_factorisation
     (cartesian_disp_functor_on_cartesian G
        (HD₂ x y f (F x xx))) (id₁ y)
     (transportf
        (λ z : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
         HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) -->[ z] G x (F x xx))
        (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)
        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))) ;; transportf
                                         (mor_disp
                                            (G y

                                            (HD₂ x y f
                                               (F x xx))))%mor_disp =

  (mor_disp (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))
     (pr1 G x (pr1 F x xx)))
  (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) f
     (id_right (id₁ y)))
  (cartesian_factorisation (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)))

        (HD₃ x y f (G x (F x xx)) ;; id_disp
                                       (G x (F x xx)))) ;;

                                         (♯ (pr1 F)

                                               xx)))%mor_disp

     (functor_comp (functor_identity C) ((pr12 C) y) f) @
   assoc (id₁ y) (id₁ y) f @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) f
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (! id_right (id₁ y)) @

xx: indexed_cat_to_psfunctor
  (cleaving_to_indexed_cat D₁ HD₁) x
! id_right f @
(id_right f @ ! id_left f) @
maponpaths (compose (id₁ y))
  (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f) @
assoc (id₁ y) (id₁ y) f @
cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) f
  (id_right (id₁ y)) =
fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f @
maponpaths (compose (id₁ y))
  (maponpaths # (functor_identity C)
     (fiber_functor_natural_data_subproof f)) @
maponpaths (compose (id₁ y))
  (functor_comp (functor_identity C) ((pr12 C) y) f) @
assoc (id₁ y) (id₁ y) f @
cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y) f
  (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y) (! id_right (id₁ y)) @
   ! id_right (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) @
   ! id_right (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y)
              (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
              (! id_left (id₁ y))))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y)
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
              (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))))) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
        (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y)
           (id₁ y) (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)))) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y · id₁ y)
     (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
        (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y))) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ y · id₁ y) (id₁ y)
     (id₁ y) (id_right (id₁ y)) @ id_right (id₁ y))

  apply homset_property.
Qed.

C: univalent_category
P₁, P₂, P₃, P₄: fib_slice_bicat C
F: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₁, P₂ ⟧
G: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₂, P₃ ⟧
H: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₃, P₄ ⟧
((# psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data F
  ◃ PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
      psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data G H)
 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
     psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data F (G · H))
• PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
    psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data
    (lassociator F G H) =
(lassociator
   (# psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data F)
   (# psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data G)

   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ x · id₁ x) (id₁ x)
     (id₁ x) (id_right (id₁ x)) @ id_right (id₁ x))
  (id_disp (pr1 H x (pr1 G x (pr1 F x xx)))) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (H x (G x (F x xx)))
     (pr1 H x (pr1 G x (pr1 F x xx))))
  (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ x) (id₁ x · id₁ x)
     (id₁ x) (! id_left (id₁ x)) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ x · id₁ x) (id₁ x)
     (id₁ x) (id_right (id₁ x)) @ id_right (id₁ x))
  (♯ H (id_disp (G x (F x xx))) ;; id_disp
                                     (H x
                                        (pr1 G x
                                           (pr1 F x xx))))%mor_disp

τ: F₁ ==> F₂
x: cat_to_bicat C^op
(PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
   psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data F₁ G
 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
     psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data (τ ▹ G)) x =
((PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
    psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data τ
  ▹ # psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data G)
 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
     psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data F₂ G) x

C: univalent_category

τ: F₁ ==> F₂
x: cat_to_bicat C^op
xx: psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data P₁ x
(PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
   psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data F₁ G
 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
     psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data (τ ▹ G)) x
  xx =
((PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
    psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data τ
  ▹ # psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data G)
 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
     psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data F₂ G) x xx

      
C: univalent_category
P₁, P₂, P₃: fib_slice_bicat C
F₁, F₂: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₁, P₂ ⟧
G: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₂, P₃ ⟧
τ: F₁ ==> F₂
x: cat_to_bicat C^op
xx: psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data P₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (pr1 G x (pr1 F₂ x xx)))
  (id_right (id₁ x))
  (id_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) ;; ♯ (pr1 G) (τ x xx))%mor_disp =
transportf
  (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (pr1 G x (pr1 F₂ x xx)))
  (id_right (id₁ x))
  (♯ G (τ x xx) ;; id_disp (G x (F₂ x xx)))%mor_disp

      
C: univalent_category
P₁, P₂, P₃: fib_slice_bicat C
F₁, F₂: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₁, P₂ ⟧
G: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₂, P₃ ⟧
τ: F₁ ==> F₂
x: cat_to_bicat C^op
xx: psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data P₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (pr1 G x (pr1 F₂ x xx)))
  (id_right (id₁ x))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (pr1 G x (pr1 F₂ x xx)))
     (id_left (id₁ x)) ((♯ (pr1 G))%mor_disp (τ x xx))) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (pr1 G x (pr1 F₂ x xx)))
  (id_right (id₁ x))
  (transportb
     (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (G x (F₂ x xx)))
     (id_right (id₁ x)) ((♯ G)%mor_disp (τ x xx)))

      
C: univalent_category
P₁, P₂, P₃: fib_slice_bicat C
F₁, F₂: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₁, P₂ ⟧
G: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₂, P₃ ⟧
τ: F₁ ==> F₂
x: cat_to_bicat C^op
xx: psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data P₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (pr1 G x (pr1 F₂ x xx)))
  (id_right (id₁ x))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (pr1 G x (pr1 F₂ x xx)))
     (! id_left (id₁ x))
     ((♯ (pr1 G))%mor_disp (τ x xx))) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (pr1 G x (pr1 F₂ x xx)))
  (id_right (id₁ x))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (G x (F₂ x xx)))
     (! id_right (id₁ x)) ((♯ G)%mor_disp (τ x xx)))

      
C: univalent_category
P₁, P₂, P₃: fib_slice_bicat C
F₁, F₂: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₁, P₂ ⟧
G: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₂, P₃ ⟧
τ: F₁ ==> F₂
x: cat_to_bicat C^op
xx: psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data P₁ x
transportf
  (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (pr1 G x (pr1 F₂ x xx)))
  (! id_left (id₁ x) @ id_right (id₁ x))
  ((♯ (pr1 G))%mor_disp (τ x xx)) =
transportf (mor_disp (G x (F₁ x xx)) (G x (F₂ x xx)))
  (! id_right (id₁ x) @ id_right (id₁ x))
  ((♯ G)%mor_disp (τ x xx))

      
C: univalent_category
P₁, P₂, P₃: fib_slice_bicat C
F₁, F₂: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₁, P₂ ⟧
G: fib_slice_bicat C ⟦ P₂, P₃ ⟧
τ: F₁ ==> F₂
x: cat_to_bicat C^op
xx: psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data P₁ x
! id_left (id₁ x) @ id_right (id₁ x) =
! id_right (id₁ x) @ id_right (id₁ x)

      apply homset_property.
  Qed.

invertible_cells psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data

C: univalent_category

  (PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
     psfunctor_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat_data F G)

      exact (property_from_invertible_2cell
               (psfunctor_comp_fib_to_psfunctor_bicat _ _ _ F G)).
  Defined.
